Section 2RURAL DEVELOPMENT AND PANCHAYAT RAJ DEPARTMENTA Government Order and Notification were issued for the restructuring and upgradation of the Harur Town Panchayat—by merging with it two Village Panchayats situated within the Harur Panchayat Union in Dharmapuri District—into a new Municipal Council. Accordingly, an Order is hereby issued, and a Notification is published in accordance with Section 15, Sub-section (4)(i) of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21/1994), for the restructuring of rural local bodies by excluding the two aforementioned Village Panchayats from the Harur Panchayat Union.Rural Development and Panchayat Raj DepartmentNotification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(w)/2026,--G.O.Ms.No. 71, Rural Development and Panchayat [Para-2(1)] Department, dated 13th March 2026.19113-03-2026Part II - Section 2Notifications or Orders of interest to a Section of the public issued by Secretariat DepartmentsA Government Order and Notification were issued for the upgradation and restructuring of Namakkal Municipality into the Namakkal Municipal Corporation, by integrating 12 Village Panchayats drawn from the Erumapatti, Mohanur, Puduchatram, and Namakkal Panchayat Unions within Namakkal District. Consequently, an Order and Notification are hereby issued—in accordance with Section 15, Sub-section (4)(i) of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21/1994)—effecting the restructuring of Rural Local Bodies by excluding the said 12 Village Panchayats situated within the Erumapatti, Mohanur, Puduchatram, and Namakkal Panchayat Unions.Rural Development and Panchayat Raj DepartmentNotificaton No. II(2)/RDPR/220(v-1)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/ 220(v-2)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(v-3)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(v-4)/2026.--G.O. Ms. No. 70, Rural Development and Panchayat [Para-2(1)] Department, dated 13th March 2026.19013-03-2026Part II - Section 2Notifications or Orders of interest to a Section of the public issued by Secretariat DepartmentsA Government Order and Notification were issued to upgrade and restructure the Pudukkottai Municipality into the Pudukkottai Municipal Corporation by fully integrating 8 Village Panchayats—and partially integrating 3 Village Panchayats—from the Thiruvarankulam, Pudukkottai, Annavasal, and Arimalam Panchayat Unions within the Pudukkottai District. Consequently, an Order and Notification are hereby issued, in accordance with Section 15, Sub-section (4)(i) of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21/1994), to restructure the Rural Local Bodies by removing—fully in the case of 8 Village Panchayats and partially in the case of 3 Village Panchayats—those entities situated within the Thiruvarankulam, Pudukkottai, Annavasal, and Arimalam Panchayat Unions.Rural Development and Panchayat Raj DepartmentNotification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(u-1)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(u-2)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(u-3)/2026, Notification No. II(2)/RDPR/220(u-4)/2026.--G.O.
